OBJECT Report 78886 Opdrachten overzicht
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=;
    Time=;
    Version List=4PS9.00.SMART.TESTEN;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    CaptionML=ENU=Opdrachten overzicht;
    OnPreReport=BEGIN
                  Counter := 0;
                  TellCounter := 0;
                  VerkoperFilter := "Try-out Quote".GETFILTER("Salesperson Code");
                  TrajectFilter := "Try-out".GETFILTER(Code);
                  EstimatorFilter := "Try-out Quote".GETFILTER(Estimator);
                  ContactNoFilter := "Try-out Quote".GETFILTER("Contact No.");
                  AllFilters := "Try-out Quote".GETFILTERS;
                  Kostenplaatsfilter := "Try-out Quote".GETFILTER("Global Dimension 1 Code");

                  //,Salesperson Code,Global Dimension 1 Code

                  IF Uitgebreid THEN BEGIN
                    CREATE(xlApp,FALSE,TRUE);
                    xlBook := xlApp.Workbooks.Add;
                    xlSheet := xlApp.Sheets.Add;
                    xlApp.DisplayAlerts := FALSE;
                    xlSheet.Name := FORMAT('Opdrachten');
                    xlSheet.Select;
                    xlSheet.Range('A1:C1').Merge;
                    xlSheet.Range('A1').Value := 'ONTVANGEN OPDRACHTEN';
                    xlSheet.Range('A4').Value := 'Status';
                    xlSheet.Range('B4').Value := 'Status trajectofferte';
                    xlSheet.Range('C4').Value := 'Traject';
                    xlSheet.Range('D4').Value := 'Hoofdtraject';
                    xlSheet.Range('E4').Value := 'Calculatie';
                    xlSheet.Range('F4').Value := 'Project';
                    xlSheet.Range('G4').Value := 'Service';
                    xlSheet.Range('H4').Value := 'Omschrijving';
                    xlSheet.Range('I4').Value := 'Bestek';
                    xlSheet.Range('J4').Value := 'Type';
                    xlSheet.Range('K4').Value := 'Kostenplaats';
                    xlSheet.Range('L4').Value := 'Offerte Nr.';
                    xlSheet.Range('M4').Value := 'Klant Nr.';
                    xlSheet.Range('N4').Value := 'Klantnaam';
                    xlSheet.Range('O4').Value := 'A,B,C,D';
                    xlSheet.Range('P4').Value := 'Naam eindklant';
                    xlSheet.Range('Q4').Value := 'A,B,C,D';
                    xlSheet.Range('R4').Value := 'Offerte datum';
                    xlSheet.Range('S4').Value := 'Geldig tot';
                    xlSheet.Range('T4').Value := 'Opdrachtdatum';
                    xlSheet.Range('U4').Value := 'Verwachte orderdatum';
                    xlSheet.Range('V4').Value := 'Planning geinformeerd';
                    xlSheet.Range('W4').Value := 'Begindatum';
                    xlSheet.Range('X4').Value := 'Einddatum';
                    xlSheet.Range('Y4').Value := 'Behandelaar';
                    xlSheet.Range('Z4').Value := 'Verkoper';
                    xlSheet.Range('AA4').Value := 'Project Manager';
                    xlSheet.Range('AB4').Value := 'Tellend';
                    xlSheet.Range('AC4').Value := 'Offertebedrag';
                    xlSheet.Range('AD4').Value := 'Kostprijs'; //leeglaten
                    xlSheet.Range('AE4').Value := 'Marge';
                    xlSheet.Range('AF4').Value := 'Verw. orderbedrag';
                    xlSheet.Range('AG4').Value := 'Kans';
                    xlSheet.Range('AH4').Value := 'OH';
                    xlSheet.Range('AI4').Value := 'Rol Peek';
                    xlSheet.Range('AJ4').Value := 'Offer Type';
                    xlSheet.Range('AK4').Value := 'Type of Work';
                    xlSheet.Range('AL4').Value := 'Category';
                    xlSheet.Range('AM4').Value := 'Products 1';
                    xlSheet.Range('AN4').Value := 'Products 1 Amount';
                    xlSheet.Range('AO4').Value := 'Products 2'; ;
                    xlSheet.Range('AP4').Value := 'Products 2 Amount';
                    xlSheet.Range('AQ4').Value := '100% offerte';
                    xlSheet.Range('AR4').Value := 'Opmerkingen';

                    xlSheet.Range('A1:AR4').Font.Bold := TRUE;
                    xlSheet.Range('A4:AR4').Interior.ColorIndex(36);

                    RowNo := 5;
                  END;
                END;

    OnPostReport=VAR
                   TempRange@1100525000 : Text[30];
                 BEGIN
                   IF Uitgebreid THEN BEGIN
                     xlSheet.Cells.Select;
                     xlSheet.Cells.EntireColumn.AutoFit ;

                     TempRange := STRSUBSTNO('A4:AR%1',RowNo - 1);
                     xlSheet.Range(TempRange).AutoFilter;

                     xlApp.Range('A5').Select;
                     xlApp.ActiveWindow.FreezePanes := TRUE;

                     xlApp.Visible := TRUE;
                     ERROR('');
                   END;
                 END;

  }
  DATASET
  {
    { 1100525000;;DataItem;PageLoop          ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number)
                                 ORDER(Ascending)
                                 WHERE(Number=CONST(1));
               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  CountRows@1100525000 : Integer;
                                BEGIN
                                END;
                                 }

    { 1100525007;1;Column;COMPANYNAME_PageLoop;
               SourceExpr=COMPANYNAME }

    { 1100525106;1;Column;Counter_PageLoop   ;
               SourceExpr=Counter }

    { 1100525107;1;Column;TellCounter_PageLoop;
               SourceExpr=TellCounter }

    { 1100525001;1;DataItem;                 ;
               DataItemTable=Table11012758;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Code);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               CurrReport.BREAK;
                             END;

               ReqFilterFields=Estimator,Contact No.,Salesperson Code,Global Dimension 1 Code,Leading }

    { 1100525002;1;DataItem;                 ;
               DataItemTable=Table11012750;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Code);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               LastFieldNo := FIELDNO(Code);
                               CheckTryOutQuotes;

                               {IF (FilterOpt <> FilterOpt::Alles) AND
                                  (FilterOpt <> FilterOpt::Leads)
                               THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;

                               IF VerkoperFilter <>'' THEN
                                 SETFILTER("Salesperson Code",VerkoperFilter);
                               IF Kostenplaatsfilter <> '' THEN
                                 SETFILTER("Global Dimension 1 Code",Kostenplaatsfilter); }
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  {IF NOT Uitgebreid AND
                                    ("Try-out"."Single/Main/Sub Tryout" = "Try-out"."Single/Main/Sub Tryout"::Main)
                                  THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  IF "Try-out Quote".GETFILTER(Leading) <> '' THEN
                                    CurrReport.SKIP;

                                  IF "Salesperson Code" <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                    SalespersonPurchaser.GET("Salesperson Code");
                                    NaamVerkoper := SalespersonPurchaser.Name;
                                  END;
                                  TrajectStatus := COPYSTR(Status,1,3);
                                  NaamEindklant := CheckEindklant(Code);
                                  Change := CheckChance(Code);

                                  IF "Expected Order Date" < WORKDATE THEN BEGIN
                                    BoldVerwOrdDatum      := "Expected Order Date";
                                    "Expected Order Date" := 0D;
                                  END ELSE BEGIN
                                    BoldVerwOrdDatum      := 0D;
                                  END;

                                  TryOutQuote.SETRANGE("Try-out No.", "Try-out".Code);

                                  PrintTryOut := (NOT TryOutQuote.FINDSET(FALSE, FALSE)) AND
                                                 (Status <= 'T70'                      );

                                  TryOutQuote.SETRANGE(Leading, TRUE);
                                  IF TryOutQuote.COUNT > 1 THEN
                                    ShowWarning := '!'
                                  ELSE
                                    ShowWarning := '';

                                  // (Uitgebreid) AND (Status = 'T00  LEAD') THEN BEGIN
                                  IF (Uitgebreid) AND (PrintTryOut) THEN BEGIN
                                    FOR ColNo := 1 TO 40 DO BEGIN
                                      CellCde[ColNo] := xl.matrix(ColNo,RowNo);
                                    END;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Value :=  TrajectStatus;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[3]).Value :=  Code;
                                    IF "Try-out"."Single/Main/Sub Tryout" <> "Try-out"."Single/Main/Sub Tryout"::Single THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[4]).Value := "Try-out"."Main Try-out"; // FORMAT("Single/Main/Sub Tryout");
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[8]).Value :=  Description;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[10]).Value := 'Lead';
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[11]).Value := FORMAT("Global Dimension 1 Code");
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[17]).Value := CheckABCD(NrEindklant);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[16]).Value := NaamEindklant;
                                    IF "Expected Order Date" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[23]).Value := "Expected Order Date";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[26]).Value :=  NaamVerkoper;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[29]).Value := "Order Amount";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[30]).Value :=  FORMAT(Change) + '%';
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[40]).Value := FORMAT(GetCommentLines(Code,TRUE));
                                    RowNo += 1;
                                  END; }
                                END;

               ReqFilterFields=Code }

    { 1100525003;1;DataItem;Opdrachtbinnen   ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               IF (FilterOpt <> FilterOpt::Alles) AND
                                  (FilterOpt <> FilterOpt::Binnen)
                               THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;

                               TempopdrBinnen.RESET;
                               IF VerkoperFilter <>'' THEN
                                 TempopdrBinnen.SETFILTER("Salesperson Code",VerkoperFilter);
                               IF EstimatorFilter <>'' THEN
                                 TempopdrBinnen.SETFILTER(Estimator,EstimatorFilter);
                               IF ContactNoFilter <>'' THEN
                                 TempopdrBinnen.SETFILTER("Contact No.",ContactNoFilter);

                               SETRANGE(Number,1,TempopdrBinnen.COUNT);
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  SalespersonPurchaser@1100525001 : Record 13;
                                  TryOutQuote@1100525000 : Record 11012758;
                                BEGIN
                                  IF Number = 1 THEN
                                    TempopdrBinnen.FINDFIRST
                                  ELSE
                                    TempopdrBinnen.NEXT;

                                  Counter += 1;

                                  Tellend := FALSE;
                                  TempopdrBinnen.CALCFIELDS("Contact Name");
                                  Ingpepland := '';
                                  EHD := '';
                                  EstimateStr := '';
                                  BoldIndienDatum := 0D;
                                  BoldAanbestDatum := 0D;
                                  NaamVerkoper := '';
                                  Behandelaar := '';

                                  TrajectStatus := COPYSTR(GetTryOutStatus(TempopdrBinnen."Try-out No."),1,3);
                                  TrjectOffStatus := COPYSTR(TempopdrBinnen.Status,1,3);
                                  ExpectedOrderDate := GetExpectedOrderDateTryOut(TempopdrBinnen."Try-out No.");

                                  IF TempopdrBinnen.Estimator <>'' THEN
                                    Behandelaar := GetBehandelaar(TempopdrBinnen.Estimator);
                                  VerwachtOrderbedrag := GetVerwachtTrajectbedrag(TempopdrBinnen.Code);
                                  Tellend := CheckLeadingOffer(TempopdrBinnen.Code);
                                  IF Tellend THEN
                                    TellCounter += 1;
                                  Change := CheckChance(TempopdrBinnen.Code);
                                  Onderhoud := CheckOnderhoud(TempopdrBinnen.Code);
                                  NaamEindklant := CheckEindklant(TempopdrBinnen."Try-out No.");
                                  Ingpepland := CheckIngepland(TempopdrBinnen.Code);
                                  EHD := CheckEHD(TempopdrBinnen."Try-out No.");
                                  EstimateStr := CheckEstimateNo(TempopdrBinnen.Code,TempopdrBinnen."Try-out No.");
                                  SoortWerk := CheckSoortwerk(TempopdrBinnen.Code);
                                  RolPeek := CheckRolPeek(TempopdrBinnen.Code);

                                  IF TempopdrBinnen."Salesperson Code" <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                    SalespersonPurchaser.GET(TempopdrBinnen."Salesperson Code");
                                    NaamVerkoper := SalespersonPurchaser.Name;
                                  END;

                                  TryOutQuote.SETRANGE("Try-out No.", TempopdrBinnen."Try-out No.");
                                  TryOutQuote.SETRANGE(Leading, TRUE);
                                  IF Tellend AND (TryOutQuote.COUNT > 1) THEN
                                    ShowWarning := '!'
                                  ELSE
                                    ShowWarning := '';

                                  IF Tellend AND (TrajectStatus <> TrjectOffStatus) THEN
                                    TrajectStatus := TrajectStatus + ' !';

                                  IF Uitgebreid THEN BEGIN
                                    FOR ColNo := 1 TO 41 DO BEGIN
                                      CellCde[ColNo] := xl.matrix(ColNo,RowNo);
                                    END;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Value := TrajectStatus;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[2]).Value := TrjectOffStatus;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[3]).Value := TempopdrBinnen."Try-out No.";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[4]).Value := EHD;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[5]).Value := EstimateStr;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[6]).Value := CheckProjectNo(TempopdrBinnen."Try-out No.",TempopdrBinnen.Code);
                                    IF MultiProj THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[6]).Interior.ColorIndex(36);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[7]).Value := CheckServiceNo(TempopdrBinnen."Try-out No.",TempopdrBinnen.Code);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[8]).Value := TempopdrBinnen.Description;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[9]).Value := TempopdrBinnen."Tender No.";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[10]).Value := 'Opdracht binnen';
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[11]).Value := TempopdrBinnen."Global Dimension 1 Code";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[12]).Value := TempopdrBinnen.Code;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[13]).Value := TempopdrBinnen."Contact No.";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[14]).Value := TempopdrBinnen."Contact Name";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[15]).Value := CheckABCD(TempopdrBinnen."Contact No.");
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[17]).Value := CheckABCD(NrEindklant);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[16]).Value := NaamEindklant;
                                    IF TempopdrBinnen."Creation Date" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[18]).Value := TempopdrBinnen."Creation Date";
                                    IF TempopdrBinnen."Apply Date" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[19]).Value := TempopdrBinnen."Apply Date";
                                    IF TempopdrBinnen."Assign Date" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[20]).Value := TempopdrBinnen."Assign Date";
                                    IF TempopdrBinnen."Register Date" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[21]).Value := TempopdrBinnen."Register Date";
                                    IF TempopdrBinnen."Tender Date" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[22]).Value := TempopdrBinnen."Tender Date";
                                    IF ExpectedOrderDate <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[23]).Value := ExpectedOrderDate;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[24]).Value := Ingpepland;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[25]).Value := Behandelaar;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[26]).Value := NaamVerkoper;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[27]).Value := TempopdrBinnen."Inserted By";
                                    IF Tellend THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[28]).Value := 'Ja' + ' ' + ShowWarning
                                    ELSE
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[28]).Value := 'Nee';
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[29]).Value := VerwachtOrderbedrag;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[30]).Value := FORMAT(Change) + '%';
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[31]).Value := Onderhoud;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[32]).Value := RolPeek;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[33]).Value := CheckOfferType(TempopdrBinnen.Code);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[34]).Value := CheckTypeOfWork(TempopdrBinnen.Code);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[35]).Value := CheckFeature(TempopdrBinnen.Code,'Category');
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[36]).Value := CheckFeature(TempopdrBinnen.Code,'Products 1');
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[37]).Value := FORMAT(CheckFeatureDec(TempopdrBinnen.Code,'Products 1'));
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[38]).Value := CheckFeature(TempopdrBinnen.Code,'Products 2'    );
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[39]).Value := FORMAT(CheckFeatureDec(TempopdrBinnen.Code,'Products 2'));
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[40]).Value := FORMAT(CheckHundredProc(TempopdrBinnen.Code));
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[41]).Value := FORMAT(GetCommentLines(TempopdrBinnen.Code,FALSE));
                                    RowNo += 1;
                                  END;

                                  IF TrjectOffStatus <= 'T10' THEN BEGIN
                                    IF TempopdrBinnen."Register Date" < TODAY THEN BEGIN
                                      BoldIndienDatum := TempopdrBinnen."Register Date";
                                      TempopdrBinnen."Register Date" := 0D;
                                      IF Uitgebreid THEN
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[21]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                    END;

                                    IF TempopdrBinnen."Register Date" < TODAY THEN BEGIN
                                      BoldAanbestDatum := TempopdrBinnen."Tender Date";
                                      TempopdrBinnen."Tender Date" := 0D;
                                      IF Uitgebreid THEN
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[22]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                    END;
                                  END;
                                  IF ExpectedOrderDate < WORKDATE THEN BEGIN
                                    BoldVerwOrdDatum  := ExpectedOrderDate;
                                    ExpectedOrderDate := 0D;
                                    IF Uitgebreid THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[23]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                  END ELSE BEGIN
                                    BoldVerwOrdDatum  := 0D;
                                  END;
                                END;
                                 }

    { 1100525112;2;Column;Number_Opdrachtbinnen;
               SourceExpr=Opdrachtbinnen.Number }

    { 1100525014;2;Column;CheckProjectNo_Opdrachtbinnen;

    { 1100525015;2;Column;CheckServiceNo_Opdrachtbinnen;
               SourceExpr=CheckServiceNo(TempopdrBinnen."Try-out No.", TempopdrBinnen.Code) }

    { 1100525016;2;Column;TempopdrBinnen_ContactName_Opdrachtbinnen;
               SourceExpr=TempopdrBinnen."Contact Name" }

    { 1100525017;2;Column;CheckABCD_TempopdrBinnen_ContactNo_Opdrachtbinnen;

    { 1100525018;2;Column;NaamEindklant_Opdrachtbinnen;

    { 1100525019;2;Column;CheckABCD_NrEindklant_Opdrachtbinnen;
               SourceExpr=CheckABCD(NrEindklant) }

    { 1100525020;2;Column;TempopdrBinnen_OrderDate_Opdrachtbinnen;
               SourceExpr=TempopdrBinnen."Order Date" }

    { 1100525021;2;Column;ExpectedOrderDate_Opdrachtbinnen;
               SourceExpr=ExpectedOrderDate }

    { 1100525022;2;Column;BoldVerwOrdDatum_Opdrachtbinnen;
               SourceExpr=BoldVerwOrdDatum }

    { 1100525023;2;Column;Ingpepland_Opdrachtbinnen;
               SourceExpr=Ingpepland }

    { 1100525024;2;Column;ProjManager_Opdrachtbinnen;
               SourceExpr=ProjManager(CheckFirstProjectNo(TempopdrBinnen."Try-out No.", TempopdrBinnen.Code)) }

    { 1100525025;2;Column;Behandelaar_Opdrachtbinnen;
               SourceExpr=Behandelaar }

    { 1100525026;2;Column;NaamVerkoper_Opdrachtbinnen;
               SourceExpr=NaamVerkoper }

    { 1100525027;2;Column;Tellend_Opdrachtbinnen;
               SourceExpr=Tellend }

    { 1100525028;2;Column;VerwachtOrderbedrag_Opdrachtbinnen;
               SourceExpr=VerwachtOrderbedrag }

    { 1100525029;2;Column;Change_Opdrachtbinnen;
               SourceExpr=Change }

    { 1100525030;2;Column;Onderhoud_Opdrachtbinnen;
               SourceExpr=Onderhoud }

    { 1100525031;2;Column;CheckHundredProc_TempopdrBinnen_Code_Opdrachtbinnen;
               SourceExpr=CheckHundredProc(TempopdrBinnen.Code) }

    { 1100525116;2;Column;ShowWarning_Opdrachtbinnen;
               OptionString='','!';
               SourceExpr=ShowWarning }

    { 1100525118;2;Column;ShowOutput1_Opdrachtbinnen;
               SourceExpr=NOT Uitgebreid }

    { 1100525119;2;Column;ShowOutput2_Opdrachtbinnen;
               SourceExpr=(NOT Uitgebreid) AND (TrajectStatus < 'T30') }

    { 1100525120;2;Column;ShowOutput3_Opdrachtbinnen;
               SourceExpr=(NOT Uitgebreid) AND (TrajectStatus >= 'T30') }

    { 1100525004;1;DataItem;OpdrOvergedragen ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               IF (FilterOpt <> FilterOpt::Alles) AND
                                  (FilterOpt <> FilterOpt::Overgedragen)
                               THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;

                               Tempopdroverrgedr.RESET;
                               IF VerkoperFilter <>'' THEN
                                 Tempopdroverrgedr.SETFILTER("Salesperson Code",VerkoperFilter);
                               IF EstimatorFilter <>'' THEN
                                 Tempopdroverrgedr.SETFILTER(Estimator,EstimatorFilter);
                               IF ContactNoFilter <>'' THEN
                                 Tempopdroverrgedr.SETFILTER("Contact No.",ContactNoFilter);

                               SETRANGE(Number,1,Tempopdroverrgedr.COUNT);
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  SalespersonPurchaser@1100525001 : Record 13;
                                  TryOutQuote@1100525000 : Record 11012758;
                                BEGIN

                                  IF Number = 1 THEN
                                    Tempopdroverrgedr.FINDFIRST
                                  ELSE
                                    Tempopdroverrgedr.NEXT;

                                  Counter += 1;

                                  Tempopdroverrgedr.CALCFIELDS("Contact Name");
                                  Tellend := FALSE;
                                  Ingpepland := '';
                                  EHD := '';
                                  EstimateStr := '';
                                  BoldIndienDatum := 0D;
                                  BoldAanbestDatum := 0D;
                                  NaamVerkoper := '';
                                  Behandelaar := '';

                                  TrajectStatus := COPYSTR(GetTryOutStatus(Tempopdroverrgedr."Try-out No."),1,3);
                                  TrjectOffStatus := COPYSTR(Tempopdroverrgedr.Status,1,3);
                                  ExpectedOrderDate := GetExpectedOrderDateTryOut(Tempopdroverrgedr."Try-out No.");

                                  IF Tempopdroverrgedr.Estimator <>'' THEN
                                    Behandelaar := GetBehandelaar(Tempopdroverrgedr.Estimator);
                                  VerwachtOrderbedrag := GetVerwachtTrajectbedrag(Tempopdroverrgedr.Code);
                                  Tellend := CheckLeadingOffer(Tempopdroverrgedr.Code);
                                  IF Tellend THEN
                                    TellCounter += 1;
                                  Change := CheckChance(Tempopdroverrgedr.Code);
                                  Onderhoud := CheckOnderhoud(Tempopdroverrgedr.Code);
                                  NaamEindklant := CheckEindklant(Tempopdroverrgedr."Try-out No.");
                                  Ingpepland := CheckIngepland(Tempopdroverrgedr.Code);
                                  EHD := CheckEHD(Tempopdroverrgedr."Try-out No.");
                                  EstimateStr := CheckEstimateNo(Tempopdroverrgedr.Code,Tempopdroverrgedr."Try-out No.");
                                  SoortWerk := CheckSoortwerk(Tempopdroverrgedr.Code);
                                  RolPeek := CheckRolPeek(Tempopdroverrgedr.Code);

                                  IF Tempopdroverrgedr."Salesperson Code" <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                    SalespersonPurchaser.GET(Tempopdroverrgedr."Salesperson Code");
                                    NaamVerkoper := SalespersonPurchaser.Name;
                                  END;

                                  IF Tellend AND (TrajectStatus <> TrjectOffStatus) THEN
                                    TrajectStatus := TrajectStatus + ' !';

                                  TryOutQuote.SETRANGE("Try-out No.", Tempopdroverrgedr."Try-out No.");
                                  TryOutQuote.SETRANGE(Leading, TRUE);
                                  IF Tellend AND (TryOutQuote.COUNT > 1) THEN
                                    ShowWarning := '!'
                                  ELSE
                                    ShowWarning := '';

                                  IF Uitgebreid THEN BEGIN
                                    FOR ColNo := 1 TO 41 DO BEGIN
                                      CellCde[ColNo] := xl.matrix(ColNo,RowNo);
                                    END;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Value := TrajectStatus;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[2]).Value := TrjectOffStatus;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[3]).Value := Tempopdroverrgedr."Try-out No.";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[4]).Value := EHD;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[5]).Value := EstimateStr;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[6]).Value := CheckProjectNo(Tempopdroverrgedr."Try-out No.",Tempopdroverrgedr.Code);
                                    IF MultiProj THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[6]).Interior.ColorIndex(36);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[7]).Value := CheckServiceNo(Tempopdroverrgedr."Try-out No.",Tempopdroverrgedr.Code);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[8]).Value := Tempopdroverrgedr.Description;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[9]).Value := Tempopdroverrgedr."Tender No.";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[10]).Value := 'Opdracht overgedragen';
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[11]).Value := Tempopdroverrgedr."Global Dimension 1 Code";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[12]).Value := Tempopdroverrgedr.Code;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[13]).Value := Tempopdroverrgedr."Contact No.";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[14]).Value := Tempopdroverrgedr."Contact Name";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[15]).Value := CheckABCD(Tempopdroverrgedr."Contact No.");
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[17]).Value := CheckABCD(NrEindklant);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[16]).Value := NaamEindklant;
                                    IF Tempopdroverrgedr."Creation Date" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[18]).Value := Tempopdroverrgedr."Creation Date";
                                    IF Tempopdroverrgedr."Apply Date" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[19]).Value := Tempopdroverrgedr."Apply Date";
                                    IF Tempopdroverrgedr."Assign Date" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[20]).Value := Tempopdroverrgedr."Assign Date";
                                    IF Tempopdroverrgedr."Register Date" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[21]).Value := Tempopdroverrgedr."Register Date";
                                    IF Tempopdroverrgedr."Tender Date" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[22]).Value := Tempopdroverrgedr."Tender Date";
                                    IF ExpectedOrderDate <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[23]).Value := ExpectedOrderDate;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[24]).Value := Ingpepland;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[25]).Value := Behandelaar;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[26]).Value := NaamVerkoper;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[27]).Value := Tempopdroverrgedr."Inserted By";
                                    IF Tellend THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[28]).Value := 'Ja'  + ' ' + ShowWarning
                                    ELSE
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[28]).Value := 'Nee';
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[29]).Value := VerwachtOrderbedrag;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[30]).Value := FORMAT(Change) + '%';
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[31]).Value := Onderhoud;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[32]).Value := RolPeek;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[33]).Value := CheckOfferType(Tempopdroverrgedr.Code);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[34]).Value := CheckTypeOfWork(Tempopdroverrgedr.Code);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[35]).Value := CheckFeature(Tempopdroverrgedr.Code,'Category');
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[36]).Value := CheckFeature(Tempopdroverrgedr.Code,'Products 1' );
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[37]).Value := FORMAT(CheckFeatureDec(Tempopdroverrgedr.Code,'Products 1' ));
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[38]).Value := CheckFeature(Tempopdroverrgedr.Code,'Products 2'    );
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[39]).Value := FORMAT(CheckFeatureDec(Tempopdroverrgedr.Code,'Products 2' ));
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[40]).Value := FORMAT(CheckHundredProc(Tempopdroverrgedr.Code));
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[41]).Value := FORMAT(GetCommentLines(Tempopdroverrgedr.Code,FALSE));
                                    RowNo += 1;
                                  END;

                                  IF TrjectOffStatus <= 'T10' THEN BEGIN
                                    IF Tempopdroverrgedr."Register Date" < TODAY THEN BEGIN
                                      BoldIndienDatum               := Tempopdroverrgedr."Register Date";
                                      Tempopdroverrgedr."Register Date" := 0D;
                                      IF Uitgebreid THEN
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[21]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                    END;

                                    IF Tempopdroverrgedr."Register Date" < TODAY THEN BEGIN
                                      BoldAanbestDatum            := Tempopdroverrgedr."Tender Date";
                                      Tempopdroverrgedr."Tender Date" := 0D;
                                      IF Uitgebreid THEN
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[22]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                    END;
                                  END;

                                  IF ExpectedOrderDate < WORKDATE THEN BEGIN
                                    BoldVerwOrdDatum  := ExpectedOrderDate;
                                    ExpectedOrderDate := 0D;
                                    IF Uitgebreid THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[23]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                  END ELSE BEGIN
                                    BoldVerwOrdDatum  := 0D;
                                  END;

                                  IF Uitgebreid AND (TrajectStatus >= 'T30') THEN BEGIN
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[2]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[3]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                  END;
                                END;
                                 }

    { 1100525005;1;DataItem;Opdrachten       ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number);
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN

                               IF (FilterOpt <> FilterOpt::Alles) AND (FilterOpt <> FilterOpt::Opdrachten) THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;

                               Tempopdrachten.RESET;
                               SETRANGE(Number,1,Tempopdrachten.COUNT);
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=VAR
                                  SalespersonPurchaser@1100525001 : Record 13;
                                  TryOutQuote@1100525000 : Record 11012758;
                                BEGIN

                                  IF Number = 1 THEN
                                    Tempopdrachten.FINDFIRST
                                  ELSE
                                    Tempopdrachten.NEXT;

                                  Counter += 1;

                                  Ingpepland := '';
                                  EHD := '';
                                  EstimateStr := '';
                                  BoldIndienDatum := 0D;
                                  BoldAanbestDatum:= 0D;
                                  NaamVerkoper := '';
                                  Behandelaar := '';

                                  Tempopdrachten.CALCFIELDS("Contact Name");
                                  Tellend := FALSE;
                                  TrajectStatus := COPYSTR(GetTryOutStatus(Tempopdrachten."Try-out No."),1,3);
                                  TrjectOffStatus := COPYSTR(Tempopdrachten.Status,1,3);
                                  ExpectedOrderDate := GetExpectedOrderDateTryOut(Tempopdrachten."Try-out No.");

                                  IF Tempopdrachten.Estimator <>'' THEN
                                    Behandelaar := GetBehandelaar(Tempopdrachten.Estimator);
                                  VerwachtOrderbedrag := GetVerwachtOrderbedrag(Tempopdrachten.Code);
                                  Tellend := CheckLeadingOffer(Tempopdrachten.Code);
                                  Change := CheckChance(Tempopdrachten.Code);
                                  Onderhoud := CheckOnderhoud(Tempopdrachten.Code);
                                  NaamEindklant := CheckEindklant(Tempopdrachten."Try-out No.");
                                  Ingpepland := CheckIngepland(Tempopdrachten.Code);
                                  EHD := CheckEHD(Tempopdrachten."Try-out No.");
                                  EstimateStr := CheckEstimateNo(Tempopdrachten.Code,Tempopdrachten."Try-out No.");
                                  SoortWerk := CheckSoortwerk(Tempopdrachten.Code);
                                  RolPeek := CheckRolPeek(Tempopdrachten.Code);

                                  IF Tempopdrachten."Salesperson Code" <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                    SalespersonPurchaser.GET(Tempopdrachten."Salesperson Code");
                                    NaamVerkoper := SalespersonPurchaser.Name;
                                  END;

                                  TryOutQuote.SETRANGE("Try-out No.", Tempopdrachten."Try-out No.");
                                  TryOutQuote.SETRANGE(Leading, TRUE);
                                  IF Tellend AND (TryOutQuote.COUNT > 1) THEN
                                    ShowWarning := '!'
                                  ELSE
                                    ShowWarning := '';

                                  IF Tellend AND (TrajectStatus <> TrjectOffStatus) THEN
                                    TrajectStatus := TrajectStatus + ' !';

                                  IF Uitgebreid THEN BEGIN
                                    FOR ColNo := 1 TO 41 DO BEGIN
                                      CellCde[ColNo] := xl.matrix(ColNo,RowNo);
                                    END;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Value := TrajectStatus;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[2]).Value := TrjectOffStatus;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[3]).Value := Tempopdrachten."Try-out No.";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[4]).Value := EHD;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[5]).Value := EstimateStr;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[6]).Value := CheckProjectNo(Tempopdrachten."Try-out No.",Tempopdrachten.Code);
                                    IF MultiProj THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[6]).Interior.ColorIndex(36);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[7]).Value := CheckServiceNo(Tempopdrachten."Try-out No.",Tempopdrachten.Code);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[8]).Value := Tempopdrachten.Description;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[9]).Value := Tempopdrachten."Tender No.";
                                  //xlSheet.Range(CellCde[10]).Value := CheckType(Tempopdrachten.Code);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[10]).Value := 'Opdrachten';
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[11]).Value := Tempopdrachten."Global Dimension 1 Code";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[12]).Value := Tempopdrachten.Code;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[13]).Value := Tempopdrachten."Contact No.";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[14]).Value := Tempopdrachten."Contact Name";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[15]).Value := CheckABCD(Tempopdrachten."Contact No.");
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[17]).Value := CheckABCD(NrEindklant);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[16]).Value := NaamEindklant;
                                    IF Tempopdrachten."Creation Date" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[18]).Value := Tempopdrachten."Creation Date";
                                    IF Tempopdrachten."Apply Date" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[19]).Value := Tempopdrachten."Apply Date";
                                    IF Tempopdrachten."Assign Date" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[20]).Value := Tempopdrachten."Assign Date";
                                    IF Tempopdrachten."Register Date" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[21]).Value := Tempopdrachten."Register Date";
                                    IF Tempopdrachten."Tender Date" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[22]).Value := Tempopdrachten."Tender Date";
                                    IF ExpectedOrderDate <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[23]).Value := ExpectedOrderDate;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[24]).Value := Ingpepland;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[25]).Value := Behandelaar;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[26]).Value := NaamVerkoper;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[27]).Value := Tempopdrachten."Inserted By";
                                    IF Tellend THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[28]).Value := 'Ja'  + ' ' + ShowWarning
                                    ELSE
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[28]).Value := 'Nee';
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[29]).Value := VerwachtOrderbedrag;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[30]).Value := FORMAT(Change) + '%';
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[31]).Value := Onderhoud;
                                   //lSheet.Range(CellCde[32]).Value := SoortWerk;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[32]).Value := RolPeek;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[33]).Value := CheckOfferType( Tempopdrachten.Code);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[34]).Value := CheckTypeOfWork(Tempopdrachten.Code);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[35]).Value := CheckFeature(Tempopdrachten.Code,'Category');
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[36]).Value := CheckFeature(Tempopdrachten.Code,'Products 1' );
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[37]).Value := FORMAT(CheckFeatureDec(Tempopdrachten.Code,'Products 1' ));
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[38]).Value := CheckFeature(Tempopdrachten.Code,'Products 2'    );
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[39]).Value := FORMAT(CheckFeatureDec(Tempopdrachten.Code,'Products 2' ));
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[40]).Value := FORMAT(CheckHundredProc(Tempopdrachten.Code));
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[41]).Value := FORMAT(GetCommentLines(Tempopdrachten.Code,FALSE));
                                    RowNo += 1;
                                  END;

                                  IF TrjectOffStatus <= 'T10' THEN BEGIN
                                    IF Tempopdrachten."Register Date" < TODAY THEN BEGIN
                                      BoldIndienDatum                          := Tempopdrachten."Register Date";
                                      Tempopdrachten."Register Date" := 0D;
                                      IF Uitgebreid THEN
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[21]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                    END;

                                    IF Tempopdrachten."Register Date" < TODAY THEN BEGIN
                                      BoldAanbestDatum                       := Tempopdrachten."Tender Date";
                                      Tempopdrachten."Tender Date" := 0D;
                                      IF Uitgebreid THEN
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[22]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                    END;
                                  END;

                                  IF ExpectedOrderDate < WORKDATE THEN BEGIN
                                    BoldVerwOrdDatum  := ExpectedOrderDate;
                                    ExpectedOrderDate := 0D;
                                    IF Uitgebreid THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[23]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                  END ELSE BEGIN
                                    BoldVerwOrdDatum  := 0D;
                                  END;

                                  IF Uitgebreid AND (TrajectStatus >= 'T30') THEN BEGIN
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[2]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[3]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                  END;
                                END;
                                 }

               SourceExpr=Opdrachten.Number }

                                  Ingpepland := CheckIngepland(TempMondelingeopd.Code);
                                  EHD := CheckEHD(TempMondelingeopd."Try-out No.");
                                  EstimateStr := CheckEstimateNo(TempMondelingeopd.Code,TempMondelingeopd."Try-out No.");
                                  SoortWerk := CheckSoortwerk(TempMondelingeopd.Code);
                                  RolPeek := CheckRolPeek(TempMondelingeopd.Code);

                                  IF TempMondelingeopd."Salesperson Code" <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                    SalespersonPurchaser.GET(TempMondelingeopd."Salesperson Code");
                                    NaamVerkoper := SalespersonPurchaser.Name;
                                  END;

                                  TryOutQuote.SETRANGE("Try-out No.", TempMondelingeopd."Try-out No.");
                                  TryOutQuote.SETRANGE(Leading, TRUE);
                                  IF Tellend AND (TryOutQuote.COUNT > 1) THEN
                                    ShowWarning := '!'
                                  ELSE
                                    ShowWarning := '';

                                    IF MultiProj THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[6]).Interior.ColorIndex(36);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[7]).Value := CheckServiceNo(TempMondelingeopd."Try-out No.",TempMondelingeopd.Code);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[8]).Value := TempMondelingeopd.Description;

                                  //xlSheet.Range(CellCde[10]).Value := CheckType(TempMondelingeopd.Code);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[10]).Value := 'Mondelinge opdrachten';
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[11]).Value := TempMondelingeopd."Global Dimension 1 Code";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[12]).Value := TempMondelingeopd.Code;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[13]).Value := TempMondelingeopd."Contact No.";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[14]).Value := TempMondelingeopd."Contact Name";
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[15]).Value := CheckABCD(TempMondelingeopd."Contact No.");
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[17]).Value := CheckABCD(NrEindklant);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[16]).Value := NaamEindklant;
                                    IF TempMondelingeopd."Creation Date" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[18]).Value := TempMondelingeopd."Creation Date";
                                    IF TempMondelingeopd."Apply Date" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[19]).Value := TempMondelingeopd."Apply Date";
                                    IF TempMondelingeopd."Assign Date" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[20]).Value := TempMondelingeopd."Assign Date";
                                    IF TempMondelingeopd."Register Date" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[21]).Value := TempMondelingeopd."Register Date";
                                    IF TempMondelingeopd."Tender Date" <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[22]).Value := TempMondelingeopd."Tender Date";
                                    IF ExpectedOrderDate <> 0D THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[23]).Value := ExpectedOrderDate;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[24]).Value := Ingpepland;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[25]).Value := Behandelaar;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[26]).Value := NaamVerkoper;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[27]).Value := TempMondelingeopd."Inserted By";
                                    IF Tellend THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[28]).Value := 'Ja'  + ' ' + ShowWarning
                                    ELSE
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[28]).Value := 'Nee';
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[29]).Value := VerwachtOrderbedrag;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[30]).Value := FORMAT(Change) + '%';
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[31]).Value := Onderhoud;
                                   //lSheet.Range(CellCde[32]).Value := SoortWerk;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[32]).Value := RolPeek;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[33]).Value := CheckOfferType( TempMondelingeopd.Code);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[34]).Value := CheckTypeOfWork(TempMondelingeopd.Code);
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[35]).Value := CheckFeature(TempMondelingeopd.Code,'Category');
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[36]).Value := CheckFeature(TempMondelingeopd.Code,'Products 1' );
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[37]).Value := FORMAT(CheckFeatureDec(TempMondelingeopd.Code,'Products 1' ));
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[38]).Value := CheckFeature(TempMondelingeopd.Code,'Products 2'    );
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[39]).Value := FORMAT(CheckFeatureDec(TempMondelingeopd.Code,'Products 2' ));
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[40]).Value := FORMAT(CheckHundredProc(TempMondelingeopd.Code));
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[41]).Value := FORMAT(GetCommentLines(TempMondelingeopd.Code,FALSE));

                                    RowNo += 1;
                                  END;

                                  IF TrjectOffStatus <= 'T10' THEN BEGIN
                                    IF TempMondelingeopd."Register Date" < TODAY THEN BEGIN
                                      BoldIndienDatum                          := TempMondelingeopd."Register Date";
                                      TempMondelingeopd."Register Date" := 0D;
                                      IF Uitgebreid THEN
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[21]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                    END;

                                    IF TempMondelingeopd."Register Date" < TODAY THEN BEGIN
                                      BoldAanbestDatum                       := TempMondelingeopd."Tender Date";
                                      TempMondelingeopd."Tender Date" := 0D;
                                      IF Uitgebreid THEN
                                        xlSheet.Range(CellCde[22]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                    END;
                                  END;

                                  IF ExpectedOrderDate < WORKDATE THEN BEGIN
                                    BoldVerwOrdDatum  := ExpectedOrderDate;
                                    ExpectedOrderDate := 0D;
                                    IF Uitgebreid THEN
                                      xlSheet.Range(CellCde[23]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                  END ELSE BEGIN
                                    BoldVerwOrdDatum  := 0D;
                                  END;

                                  IF Uitgebreid AND (TrajectStatus >= 'T30') THEN BEGIN
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[1]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[2]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                    xlSheet.Range(CellCde[3]).Font.Bold := TRUE;
                                  END;
                                END;
                                 }

    PROCEDURE CheckTryOutQuotes@1000000017();
    VAR
      TryOutQuote@1000000000 : Record 11012758;
      TryOut@1000000001 : Record 11012750;
      SkipBl@1000000002 : Boolean;
    BEGIN
      IF AllFilters <>'' THEN
        TryOutQuote.COPYFILTERS("Try-out Quote");
      IF TrajectFilter <> '' THEN
        TryOutQuote.SETFILTER("Try-out No.",TrajectFilter);
      IF TryOutQuote.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        IF (TryOut.GET(TryOutQuote."Try-out No.")) AND
           (TryOut."Single/Main/Sub Tryout" = TryOut."Single/Main/Sub Tryout"::Main)
        THEN
          EXIT;
        REPEAT
          IF (TryOutQuote."Order Date" <> 0D) AND (TryOutQuote."Order Date" < (TODAY - 90)) THEN
            SkipBl := TRUE
          ELSE
            CASE TryOutQuote.Status OF
              //Toe te wijzen - Opdracht binnen
              'T30  ORDER':FillTempopdrBinnen(TryOutQuote);
              //Aanvragen - OPDRACHT OVERGEDRAGEN
              'T40  HANDED OVER'  :FillTempopdroverrgedr(TryOutQuote);
              //Uitgebrachte offertes - OPDRACHTEN
              'T45  PROJECT STARTED':FillTempopdrachten(TryOutQuote);
              //Hold  - Mondeling oprdrachten
              'T25  VERBAL ORDER': FillTempMondelingeopd(TryOutQuote);
            END;
        UNTIL TryOutQuote.NEXT = 0;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckEindklant@1000000104(TryoutQuoteNo@1000000001 : Code[20]) : Text[50];
    VAR
      TryOutLine@1000000000 : Record 11012755;
    BEGIN
      TryOutLine.SETRANGE("Try-out No.",TryoutQuoteNo);
      TryOutLine.SETFILTER("Contact Type",'END CUSTOMER');
      IF TryOutLine.COUNT > 1 THEN
        ERROR(Text003,TryoutQuoteNo);
      IF TryOutLine.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
        NrEindklant := TryOutLine."Contact No.";
        TryOutLine.CALCFIELDS("Contact Name");
        EXIT(TryOutLine."Contact Name");
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckProjectNo@1000000142(tryout@1000000001 : Code[20];tryoutquote@1000000002 : Code[20]) : Code[20];
    VAR
      TryoutSuccessor@1000000000 : Record 11012761;
    BEGIN
      MultiProj := FALSE;
      TryoutSuccessor.SETRANGE("Try-out No.",tryout);
      TryoutSuccessor.SETRANGE("Try-out Quote",tryoutquote);
      TryoutSuccessor.SETFILTER("Project No.",'<>%1','');
      IF TryoutSuccessor.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        IF TryoutSuccessor.COUNT > 1 THEN BEGIN
          MultiProj := TRUE;
          EXIT(STRSUBSTNO('[%1]', TryoutSuccessor.COUNT));
        END ELSE IF TryoutSuccessor.FINDFIRST THEN
          EXIT(TryoutSuccessor."Project No.");
      END ELSE
        EXIT('');
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckServiceNo@1000000143(tryout@1000000001 : Code[20];tryoutquote@1000000002 : Code[20]) : Code[20];
    VAR
      TryoutSuccessor@1000000000 : Record 11012761;
    BEGIN
      MultiServ := FALSE;
      TryoutSuccessor.SETRANGE("Try-out No.",tryout);
      TryoutSuccessor.SETRANGE("Try-out Quote",tryoutquote);
      TryoutSuccessor.SETFILTER("Service Order No.",'<>%1','');
      IF TryoutSuccessor.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        IF TryoutSuccessor.COUNT > 1 THEN BEGIN
          MultiServ := TRUE;
          EXIT(STRSUBSTNO('[%1]', TryoutSuccessor.COUNT));
        END ELSE IF TryoutSuccessor.FINDFIRST THEN
          EXIT(TryoutSuccessor."Service Order No.");
      END ELSE BEGIN
        TryoutSuccessor.SETRANGE("Service Order No.");
        TryoutSuccessor.SETFILTER("Service Contract No.",'<>%1','');
        IF TryoutSuccessor.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
          IF TryoutSuccessor.COUNT > 1 THEN
            MultiServ := TRUE;
          IF TryoutSuccessor.FINDFIRST THEN
            EXIT(TryoutSuccessor."Service Contract No.");
        END ELSE BEGIN
          TryoutSuccessor.SETRANGE("Service Contract No.");
          TryoutSuccessor.SETFILTER("Service Location No.",'<>%1','');
          IF TryoutSuccessor.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
            IF TryoutSuccessor.COUNT > 1 THEN
              MultiServ := TRUE;
            IF TryoutSuccessor.FINDFIRST THEN
              EXIT(TryoutSuccessor."Service Location No.");
          END ELSE
            EXIT('');
        END;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckEHD@1000000030(TrajectNo@1000000000 : Code[20]) : Text[50];

    PROCEDURE CheckEstimateNo@1000000045(TrajectOffNo@1000000000 : Code[20];TrajectNo@1000000002 : Code[20]) : Text[250];
    VAR
      TryoutSuccessor@1000000001 : Record 11012761;
      TempStr@1000000003 : Text[1024];
    BEGIN
      // JvL TempStr from 50 --> 1024 characters
      TryoutSuccessor.SETRANGE("Try-out No.",TrajectNo);
      TryoutSuccessor.SETRANGE("Try-out Quote",TrajectOffNo);
      TryoutSuccessor.SETFILTER("Estimate No.",'<>%1','');
      IF TryoutSuccessor.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          IF TempStr = '' THEN
            TempStr := TryoutSuccessor."Estimate No."
          ELSE
            TempStr := TempStr + STRSUBSTNO(', %1',TryoutSuccessor."Estimate No.");
        UNTIL TryoutSuccessor.NEXT = 0;
        EXIT(TempStr);
      END ELSE
        EXIT('');
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckFeature@1000000001(TryOutQuoteNo@1000000000 : Code[20];Feature@1000000002 : Code[20]) : Text[30];
    VAR
      ContactFeatureType@1000000001 : Record 11012753;
    BEGIN

    PROCEDURE GetCommentLines@1000000004(Code@1000000000 : Code[20];Traject@1000000001 : Boolean) : Text[500];
    VAR
      CommentLineRec@1000000002 : Record 97;
      TempText@1000000003 : Text[500];
    BEGIN
      IF Traject THEN
        CommentLineRec.SETRANGE("Table Name", CommentLineRec."Table Name"::"Try-out")
      ELSE
        CommentLineRec.SETRANGE("Table Name", CommentLineRec."Table Name"::"Try-out Quote");

      CommentLineRec.SETRANGE("No.", Code);
      IF CommentLineRec.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
        REPEAT
          IF TempText = '' THEN
            TempText := CommentLineRec.Comment
          ELSE
            TempText := TempText + ' - ' + CommentLineRec.Comment;
        UNTIL CommentLineRec.NEXT = 0;
      END;

      EXIT(TempText);
    END;

    PROCEDURE ProjManager@1000000003(JobNo@1000000000 : Code[20]) : Text[50];
    VAR
      JobRec@1000000001 : Record 11072003;
    BEGIN
      //ProjManager(CheckProjectNo(TempopdrBinnen."Try-out No.", TempopdrBinnen.Code))
      IF JobNo <> '' THEN BEGIN
        IF JobRec.GET(JobNo) THEN BEGIN
          JobRec.CALCFIELDS("Name Project Manager");
          EXIT(JobRec."Name Project Manager");
        END;
      END;
    END;

    END;

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value = 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &gt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt; 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    if Value &lt;= 0 then
        Return ""
    end if
    Return Value
End Function
